<p>Apart from the similarities between forms highlighted in <b>bold</b>, it will be observed that all basic forms start with <i>v-</i> except for the 3rd person plural intransitive forms, that all basic <i>transitive</i> indicative forms have <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/a/</span> as their first vowel, that all basic <i>intransitive</i> indicative forms have <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/u/</span> as their first vowel (<i>voq</i> is phonemically <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/vuq/</span>), and that all basic forms unique to the interrogative mood have <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/i/</span> as their first vowel except for the 3rd person intransitive forms. Furthermore, if the subject of a transitive verb is 3rd person, the suffix will start with <i>vaa-</i> (with one exception). In the forms unique to the interrogative transitive (which all have 2nd person subjects), the forms with a (2nd person) <i>singular</i> subject are turned into forms with a (2nd person) <i>plural</i> subject by adding <i>-si-</i> after the initial <i>vi-</i> (except when the object is 1st person plural, in which case the same form is used for both plural and singular subject, as is the case for all indicative and interrogative forms with the object in the 1st or 2nd person plural). When the object is 1st or 2nd person singular, the forms with a 3rd person <i>singular</i> subject are turned into forms with a (3rd person) <i>plural</i> subject by lengthening the second consonant: <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">[vaːŋa]</span> → <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">[vaːŋŋa]</span>, <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">[vaːt͡sit̚]</span> → <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">[vaːtt͡sit̚]</span>. If the subject or object is 2nd person plural, the suffix will include <i>-si(-)</i>. If the subject or object is 1st person plural, the suffix will end in <i>-t</i> except when the object is 2nd person plural.
</p><p>The interrogative mood has separate forms only when the subject is 2nd person or intransitive 3rd person; otherwise, the interrogative forms are identical to the indicative forms. All suffixes that start with <i>vi-</i> have a subject in the 2nd person.
</p><p>The initial <i>v-</i> changes to <i>p-</i> or is deleted according to the rules described <a href="#Rules">above</a>.
</p><p>After the suffix <i>-nngil-</i> ‘not’, <i>v-</i> is deleted (while the <i>pp-</i> of the 3rd person plural intransitive forms is changed to <i>l-</i>) and a first vowel <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/u/</span> is changed to <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/a/</span> (e.g. <i>suli+vugut</i> ‘we work’ but <i>suli-nngil+agut</i> ‘we don't work’). The intransitive 2nd person does not have separate interrogative forms after <i>-nngil-</i>, hence e.g.
</p>
<ul><li><i>suli+vutit</i> ‘you (sg.) work’</li>
<li><i>suli-nngil+atit</i> ‘you (sg.) don't work’</li>
<li><i>suli+vit?</i> ‘do you (sg.) work?’</li>
<li><i>suli-nngil+atit?</i> ‘don't you (sg.) work?’ (instead of the expected *<i>suli-nngil+it?</i>)</li></ul>
<p>After the future suffix <i>-ssa-</i>, <i>vu-</i> and <i>vo-</i> (both <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/vu/</span>) change to <i>a-</i>. (<i>Va-</i>, <i>vi-</i>, <i>ppu-</i>, and <i>ppa-</i> do not change.)
</p><p>After the suffix <i>-qa-</i> ‘very’, <i>vu-</i>, <i>vo-</i>, <i>va-</i>, <i>vi-</i>, <i>ppu-</i>, and <i>ppa-</i> all change to <i>a-</i> (except when this would lead to <i>aaa</i>, in which case <i>aaa</i> is shortened to <i>aa</i>). <i>-qa-</i> + <i>vai</i> becomes <i>qai</i>, not *<i>qaai</i>. (In accordance with the <a href="#Rule">rule</a>, <i>aau</i> becomes <i>aaju</i>, hence <i>-qa-</i> + <i>viuk</i> becomes <i>qaajuk</i>, not *<i>qaauk</i>.) The suffix <i>-qa-</i> was historically <i>-qi-</i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Imperative_and_optative_moods">Imperative and optative moods</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Imperative and optative moods"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>The imperative mood is used to issue orders and is always combined with the second person. The optative is used to express wishes or exhortations and is never used with the second person. There is a negative imperative form used to issue prohibitions. Both optative and imperative have transitive and intransitive paradigms. There are two transitive positive imperative paradigms: a standard one and another that is considered rude and is used usually to address children.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">sini-git!</p><p style="margin: 0px;">sleep-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="imperative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IMP</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">sini-git!</p><p style="display: none;">sleep-IMP</p><p style="clear: left;">"Sleep!"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">sini-llanga</p><p style="margin: 0px;">sleep-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="optative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">OPT</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">sini-llanga</p><p style="display: none;">sleep-1.OPT</p><p style="clear: left;">"Let me sleep!"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">sini-nnak!</p><p style="margin: 0px;">sleep-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="negation/negative" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">NEG</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="imperative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IMP</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">sini-nnak!</p><p style="display: none;">sleep-NEG.IMP</p><p style="clear: left;">"Don't sleep!"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Conditional_mood">Conditional mood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Conditional mood"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Conditional_mood" title="Conditional mood">conditional mood</a> is used to construct subordinate clauses that mean "if" or "when".<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">seqinner-pat</p><p style="margin: 0px;">sunshine-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="conditional mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">COND</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Eva</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Eva</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">ani-ssaa-q</p><p style="margin: 0px;">go out-expect/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">seqinner-pat Eva ani-ssaa-q</p><p style="display: none;">sunshine-COND Eva {go out}-expect/3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"If the sun shines, Eva will go out"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Causative_mood">Causative mood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Causative mood"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Causative_mood" title="Causative mood">causative mood</a> (sometimes called the <i>conjunctive</i>) is used to construct subordinate clauses that mean "because", "since" or "when" and is also sometimes used to mean "that". The causative is used also in main clauses to imply some underlying cause.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qasu-gami</p><p style="margin: 0px;">be tired-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="causative mood&lt;/div&gt;" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CAU</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">innar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">go to bed-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">qasu-gami innar-poq</p><p style="display: none;">{be tired}-CAU/3SG {go to bed}-3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"He went to bed because he was tired"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">matta-ttor-ama</p><p style="margin: 0px;">blubber-eat-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="causative mood&lt;/div&gt;" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CAU</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">matta-ttor-ama</p><p style="display: none;">blubber-eat-CAU/1SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"I've eaten blubber (that's why I'm not hungry)"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">ani-guit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">go out-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="conditional mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">COND</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="second person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">2SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">eqqaama-ssa-vat</p><p style="margin: 0px;">remember-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="future tense" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">FUT</abbr>-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="imperative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IMP</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">teriannia-qar-mat</p><p style="margin: 0px;">fox-are-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="causative" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CAUS</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">ani-guit eqqaama-ssa-vat teriannia-qar-mat</p><p style="display: none;">{go out}-COND/2SG remember-FUT-IMP fox-are-CAUS</p><p style="clear: left;">"If you go out, remember that there are foxes"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Contemporative_mood">Contemporative mood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Contemporative mood"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>The contemporative mood is used to construct subordinate clauses with the meaning of simultaneity and is used only if the subject of the subordinate clause and of the main clause are identical. If they differ, the participial mood or the causative mood is used. The contemporative can also be used to form complement clauses for verbs of speaking or thinking.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qasu-llunga</p><p style="margin: 0px;">be tired-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="contemporative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CONT</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">angerlar-punga</p><p style="margin: 0px;">go.home-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">qasu-llunga angerlar-punga</p><p style="display: none;">{be tired}-CONT.1SG go.home-1SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"Being tired, I went home"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">98-inik</p><p style="margin: 0px;">98-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="plural number" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">ukio-qar-luni</p><p style="margin: 0px;">year-have-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="contemporative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CONT</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="fourth (reflexive or obviative) person" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">4</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="singular number" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">toqu-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">die-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">98-inik ukio-qar-luni toqu-voq</p><p style="display: none;">98-INSTR.PL year-have-CONT.4.SG die-3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"Being 98 years old, he/she died", "he/she was 98 when he/she died"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Eva</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Eva</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">oqar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">say-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kami-it</p><p style="margin: 0px;">boot-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="plural number" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">akiler-lugit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">pay-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="contemporative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CONT</abbr>.<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, plural" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3PL</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Eva oqar-poq kami-it akiler-lugit</p><p style="display: none;">Eva say-3SG boot-PL pay-CONT.3PL</p><p style="clear: left;">"Eva said she had paid for the boots"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Participial_mood">Participial mood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Participial mood"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>The participial mood is used to construct a subordinate clause describing its subject in the state of carrying out an activity. It is used when the matrix clause and the subordinate clause have different subjects. It is often used in appositional phrases such as <a href="/wiki/Relative_clauses" class="mw-redirect" title="Relative clauses">relative clauses</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">atuar-toq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">read-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="participial mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PART</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">taku-ara</p><p style="margin: 0px;">see-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">atuar-toq taku-ara</p><p style="display: none;">read-PART/3SG see-1SG/3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"I saw her read/I saw that she read"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">neriu-ppunga</p><p style="margin: 0px;">hope-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">tiki-ssa-soq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">come-expect-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="participial mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PART</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">neriu-ppunga tiki-ssa-soq</p><p style="display: none;">hope-1SG come-expect-PART/3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"I hope he is coming/I hope he'll come"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derivation">Derivation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Derivation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Verbal derivation is extremely productive, and Greenlandic has many hundreds of derivational suffixes. Often, a single verb uses more than one derivational suffix, resulting in very long words. Here are some examples of how derivational suffixes can change the meaning of verbs:
</p>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-katak-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"be tired of"</p></div><p style="display: none;">-katak-</p><p style="display: none;">{"be tired of"}</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</th>
<td><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">taku-katap-para</p><p style="margin: 0px;">see-tired.of-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">1SG</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">taku-katap-para</p><p style="display: none;">see-tired.of-1SG/3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"I am tired of seeing it/him/her</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>

</div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Time_reference_and_aspect">Time reference and aspect</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Time reference and aspect"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Greenlandic grammar has morphological devices to mark a distinction between the recent and distant past, but their use is optional<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> and so they should be understood as parts of Greenlandic's extensive derivational system, rather than as a system of <a href="/wiki/Tense_(grammar)" class="mw-redirect" title="Tense (grammar)">tense</a>-markers. Rather than by morphological marking, fixed temporal distance is expressed by temporal adverbials:<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">toqo-riikatap-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">die-long.ago-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">toqo-riikatap-poq</p><p style="display: none;">die-long.ago-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"He died long ago"<sup id="cite_ref-Fortescue_1984_p._273_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fortescue_1984_p._273-72">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">nere-qqammer-punga</p><p style="margin: 0px;">eat-recently-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular">1sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">nere-qqammer-punga</p><p style="display: none;">eat-recently-1sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"I ate recently"<sup id="cite_ref-Fortescue_1984_p._273_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fortescue_1984_p._273-72">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">ippassaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">yesterday</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Piitaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Peter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">arpap-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">run-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">ippassaq Piitaq arpap-poq</p><p style="display: none;">yesterday Peter-ABS run-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"Yesterday Peter was running."<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._174_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._174-73">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>All other things being equal and in the absence of any explicit adverbials, the indicative mood is interpreted as complete or incomplete, depending on the verbal <a href="/wiki/Lexical_aspect" title="Lexical aspect">lexical aspect</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._174_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._174-73">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Piitaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Peter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">arpap-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">run-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Piitaq arpap-poq</p><p style="display: none;">Peter-ABS run-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"Peter runs"<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._174_73-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._174-73">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Piitaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Peter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">ani-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">go.out-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Piitaq ani-voq</p><p style="display: none;">Peter-ABS go.out-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"Peter was gone out"<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._174_73-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._174-73">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>However, if a sentence with an atelic verbal phrase is embedded within the context of a past-time narrative, it would be interpreted as past.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Greenlandic has several purely-derivational devices of expressing meaning related to aspect and lexical aspect such as <i>sar</i>, expressing "habituality", and <span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">ssaar</i></span>, expressing, "stop to".<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Also, there are at least two major perfect markers: <i>sima</i> and <i>nikuu</i>. <i>sima</i> can occur in several positions with obviously-different functions.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The last position indicates evidential meaning, but that can be determined only if several suffixes are present.
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">tiki(k)-nikuu-sima-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">arrive-<b>nikuu-sima</b>-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="intransitive" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INT</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">tiki(k)-nikuu-sima-voq</p><p style="display: none;">arrive-<b>nikuu-sima</b>-3sg/INT</p><p style="clear: left;">"Apparently, she had arrived"<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>With <a href="/wiki/Telicity" title="Telicity">atelic verbs</a>, there is a regular contrast between indirective <a href="/wiki/Evidentiality" title="Evidentiality">evidentiality</a>, marked by <i>sima</i>, and witnessed evidentiality, marked by <i>nikuu</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._179_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._179-78">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Its evidential meaning causes the combination of first person and <i>sima</i> to be sometimes marked.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qia-sima-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">cry-<b>sima</b>-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">qia-sima-voq</p><p style="display: none;">cry-<b>sima</b>-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"He cried (his eyes are swollen)"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qia-nikuu-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">cry-<b>nikuu</b>-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">qia-nikuu-voq</p><p style="display: none;">cry-<b>nikuu</b>-3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"He cried (I was there)"<sup id="cite_ref-Trondhjem_2009_p._179_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trondhjem_2009_p._179-78">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>In the written language<sup id="cite_ref-Fortescue_1984_p._273_72-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fortescue_1984_p._273-72">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> and more recently also in the spoken language, especially by younger speakers, <i>sima</i> and <i>nikuu</i> can be used together with adverbials to refer to a particular time in the past.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> That is, they can arguably mark time reference but do not yet do so systematically.
</p><p>Just as Greenlandic does not systematically mark past tense, the language also does not have a future tense. Rather, it employs three different strategies to express future meaning:
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">1)</div><div>suffixes denoting cognitive states that show an attitude about prospective actions</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Ilimaga-ara</p><p style="margin: 0px;">expect-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular">1sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">aasaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">summer</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">manna</p><p style="margin: 0px;">this</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Dudley</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Dudley</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qujanar-tor-si-ffigi-ssa-llugu</p><p style="margin: 0px;">be.fun-cn-get.from-expect-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="contemporative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">CONT</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Ilimaga-ara aasaq manna Dudley qujanar-tor-si-ffigi-ssa-llugu</p><p style="display: none;">expect-1sg/3sg/IND summer this Dudley be.fun-cn-get.from-expect-CONT/3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"I expect to get some fun out of Dudley this summer."</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">2)</div><div>inchoative suffixes creating telic actions that can then be understood as already having begun by virtue of the indicative mood</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Aggiuti-ler-para</p><p style="margin: 0px;">bring-begin-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular">1sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Aggiuti-ler-para</p><p style="display: none;">bring-begin-1sg/3sg/IND</p><p style="clear: left;">"I've started to bring him."</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">3)</div><div>moods that mark the speech act as a request or wish<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Qimmii-t</p><p style="margin: 0px;">dog-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="plural number" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">nerisi(k)-tigit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">feed-please-we/them/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="imperative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IMP</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Qimmii-t nerisi(k)-tigit</p><p style="display: none;">dog-PL feed-please-we/them/IMP</p><p style="clear: left;">"Let us feed the dogs, ok?"<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The status of the perfect markers as aspect is not very controversial, but some scholars have claimed that Greenlandic has a basic temporal distinction between future and <a href="/wiki/Nonfuture_tense" title="Nonfuture tense">nonfuture</a>. Especially, the suffix <i>-ssa</i> and handful of other suffixes have been claimed to be obligatory future markers.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> However, at least for literary Greenlandic, the suffixes have been shown to have other semantics, which can be used to refer to the future by the strategies that have just been described.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voice">Voice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Voice"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Greenlandic has an <a href="/wiki/Antipassive_voice" title="Antipassive voice">antipassive voice</a>, which transforms the ergative subject into an absolutive subject and the absolutive object into an instrumental argument; it is formed mostly by the addition of the marker <i>-(s)i-</i> to the verb (the presence of the consonant being mostly phonologically determined, albeit with a few cases of lexically determined distribution) and, in small lexically restricted sets of verbs, by the addition of <i>-nnig-</i> or <i>-ller-</i> (the former being, however, more frequent because it is the one selected by the common verbal element <i>-gi/ri-</i> 'to have as').<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> It has also been analysed as having <a href="/wiki/Passive_voice" title="Passive voice">passive voice</a> constructions, which are formed with the elements <i>-saa-</i> (composed of the passive participle suffix <i>-sa-</i> and <i>-u-</i> 'to be'), <i>-neqar-</i> (composed of the verbal noun suffix <i>-neq-</i> and <i>-qar-</i> 'to have') and <i>-tit-</i> (only to demote higher animate participants, also used with a reflexive causative meaning 'to cause, let [someone do something to one]'). In addition, an "impersonal passive" from intransitive verbs <i>-toqar-</i> (composed of intransitive agent suffix <i>-toq-</i> and <i>-qar</i> 'to have') has been identified.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_incorporation">Noun incorporation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Noun incorporation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>There is also a debate in the linguistic literature on whether Greenlandic has <a href="/wiki/Noun_incorporation" class="mw-redirect" title="Noun incorporation">noun incorporation</a>. The language does not allow the kind of incorporation that common in many other languages in which a noun root can be incorporated into almost any verb to form a verb with a new meaning. On the other hand, Greenlandic often forms verbs that include noun roots. The question then becomes whether to analyse such verb formations as incorporation or as denominal derivation of verbs. Greenlandic has a number of <a href="/wiki/Morpheme" title="Morpheme">morphemes</a> that require a noun root as their host and form <a href="/wiki/Complex_predicate" class="mw-redirect" title="Complex predicate">complex predicates</a>, which correspond closely in meaning to what is often seen in languages that have canonical noun incorporation. Linguists who propose that Greenlandic had incorporation argue that such morphemes are in fact verbal roots, which must incorporate nouns to form grammatical clauses.<sup id="cite_ref-Sadock_2003_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sadock_2003-53">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> That argument is supported by the fact that many of the derivational morphemes that form denominal verbs work almost identically to canonical noun incorporation. They allow the formation of words with a semantic content that correspond to an entire English clause with verb, subject and object. Another argument is that the morphemes that derive denominal verbs come from historical noun incorporating constructions, which have become fossilized.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Other linguists maintain that the morphemes in question are simply derivational morphemes that allow the formation of denominal verbs. That argument is supported by the fact that the morphemes are always latched on to a nominal element.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> These examples illustrate how Greenlandic forms complex predicates including nominal roots:
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qimmeq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"dog"</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">+</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-qar-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"have"</p></div><p style="display: none;">qimmeq + -qar-</p><p style="display: none;">"dog" {} "have"</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kaffi</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"coffee"</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">+</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-sor-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"drink/eat"</p></div><p style="display: none;">kaffi + -sor-</p><p style="display: none;">"coffee" {} "drink/eat"</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</th>
<td><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kaffi-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">coffee</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-sor-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">drink/eat</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;"><abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">kaffi- -sor- -poq</p><p style="display: none;">coffee drink/eat 3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"She drinks coffee"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">puisi</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"seal"</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">+</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-nniar-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"hunt"</p></div><p style="display: none;">puisi + -nniar-</p><p style="display: none;">"seal" {} "hunt"</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</th>
<td><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">puisi-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">seal</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-nniar-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">hunt</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;"><abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">puisi- -nniar- -poq</p><p style="display: none;">seal hunt 3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"She hunts seal"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">allagaq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"letter"</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">+</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-si-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"receive"</p></div><p style="display: none;">allagaq + -si-</p><p style="display: none;">"letter" {} "receive"</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</th>
<td><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">allagar-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">letter</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-si-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">receive</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;"><abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">allagar- -si- -voq</p><p style="display: none;">letter receive 3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"She has received a letter"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">anaana</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"mother"</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">+</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-a-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">"to be"</p></div><p style="display: none;">anaana + -a-</p><p style="display: none;">"mother" {} {"to be"}</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</th>
<td><div class="interlinear"><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">anaana-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">mother</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-a-</p><p style="margin: 0px;">to be</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;"><abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">anaana- -a- -voq</p><p style="display: none;">mother {to be} 3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"She is a mother"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nouns">Nouns</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Nouns"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Nouns are always inflected for case and number and sometimes for number and person of possessor. Singular and plural are distinguished and eight cases are used: absolutive, ergative (relative), instrumental, allative, locative, ablative, prosecutive (also called vialis or prolative) and equative.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> Case and number are marked by a single suffix. Nouns can be derived from verbs or from other nouns by a number of suffixes: <span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">atuar</i></span>- "to read" + -<span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">fik</i></span> "place" becomes <span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">atuarfik</i></span> "school" and <span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">atuarfik</i></span> + -<span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">tsialak</i></span> "something good" becomes <span title="Greenlandic-language text"><i lang="kl">atuarfitsialak</i></span> "good school".
</p><p>Since the possessive agreement suffixes on nouns and the transitive agreement suffixes on verbs in a number of instances have similar or identical shapes, there is even a theory that Greenlandic distinguishes between transitive and intransitive nouns as it does for verbs.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;j&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronouns">Pronouns</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Pronouns"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>There are personal pronouns for first, second, and third person singular and plural. They are optional as subjects or objects but only when the verbal inflection refers to such arguments.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align: center;">
<caption>Personal pronouns
</caption>
<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">
</th>
<th scope="col">Singular
</th>
<th scope="col">Plural
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">1st person
</th>
<td>uanga</td>
<td>uagut
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">2nd person
</th>
<td>illit</td>
<td>ilissi
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">3rd person
</th>
<td>una</td>
<td>uku
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Personal pronouns are, however, required in the oblique case:
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">illit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">you</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">nere-qu-aatit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">eat-tell to-3s–2s-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="indicative mood" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">IND</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">illit nere-qu-aatit</p><p style="display: none;">you {eat-tell to-3s–2s-IND}</p><p style="clear: left;">'He told you to eat'</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Case">Case</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Case"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Both grammatical core cases, ergative and absolutive, are used to express grammatical and syntactical roles of participant noun phrases. The oblique cases express information related to movement and manner.
</p>
<table class="wikitable" style="margin: 0 0 0 1em; float: right;">
<caption><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1126788409"><div class="plainlist"><ul><li>3. Kalaallisut</li><li>case endings</li></ul></div>
</caption>
<tbody><tr>
<th>case
</th>
<th>singular
</th>
<th>plural
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th>Absolutive
</th>
<td>-Ø
</td>
<td>-(i)t
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Ergative
</th>
<td>-(u)p
</td>
<td>-(i)t
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumental
</th>
<td>-mik
</td>
<td>-nik
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Allative
</th>
<td>-mut
</td>
<td>-nut
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Locative
</th>
<td>-mi
</td>
<td>-ni
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Ablative
</th>
<td>-mit
</td>
<td>-nit
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Prosecutive
</th>
<td>-kkut
</td>
<td>-tigut
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>-tut
</td>
<td>-tut
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">angut-Ø</p><p style="margin: 0px;">man-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">neri-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">eat-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">angut-Ø neri-voq</p><p style="display: none;">man-ABS eat-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"The man eats"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">anguti-p</p><p style="margin: 0px;">man-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="ergative case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ERG</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">puisi</p><p style="margin: 0px;">seal-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">neri-vaa</p><p style="margin: 0px;">eat-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">anguti-p puisi neri-vaa</p><p style="display: none;">man-ERG seal-ABS eat-3sg/3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"The man eats the seal"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Instrumental_case" title="Instrumental case">instrumental case</a> is versatile. It is used for the instrument with which an action is carried out, for oblique objects of intransitive verbs (also called <a href="/wiki/Antipassive" class="mw-redirect" title="Antipassive">antipassive</a> verbs)<sup id="cite_ref-Sadock_2003_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sadock_2003-53">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> and for secondary objects of transitive verbs.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">nanoq-Ø</p><p style="margin: 0px;">polar bear-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">savim-mi-nik</p><p style="margin: 0px;">knife-his.own-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kapi-vaa</p><p style="margin: 0px;">stab-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">nanoq-Ø savim-mi-nik kapi-vaa</p><p style="display: none;">{polar bear}-ABS knife-his.own-INSTR stab-3sg/3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"He stabbed the bear with his knife"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Piitaq-Ø</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Peter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="absolutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">savim-mik</p><p style="margin: 0px;">knife-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">tuni-vara</p><p style="margin: 0px;">give-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="first person, singular">1sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Piitaq-Ø savim-mik tuni-vara</p><p style="display: none;">Peter-ABS knife-INSTR give-1sg/3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"I gave Peter a knife"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>There is no case marking if the noun is incorporated. Many sentences can be constructed oblique object as well as incorporated object.
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kaffi-sor-tar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">coffee-drink-usually-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">kaffi-sor-tar-poq</p><p style="display: none;">coffee-drink-usually-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"She usually drinks coffee"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kaffi-mik</p><p style="margin: 0px;">coffee-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">imer-tar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">drink-usually-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">kaffi-mik imer-tar-poq</p><p style="display: none;">coffee-INSTR drink-usually-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"She usually drinks coffee"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>It is also used to express the meaning of "give me" and to form adverbs from nouns:
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">imer-mik!</p><p style="margin: 0px;">water-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">imer-mik!</p><p style="display: none;">water-INSTR</p><p style="clear: left;">"(give me) water"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">sivisuu-mik</p><p style="margin: 0px;">late-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="instrumental case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">INSTR</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">sinip-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">sleep-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">sivisuu-mik sinip-poq</p><p style="display: none;">late-INSTR sleep-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"He slept late"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Allative_case" title="Allative case">allative case</a> describes movement towards something.<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase-104">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">illu-mut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">house-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="allative case (&#39;to&#39;)" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ALL</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">illu-mut</p><p style="display: none;">house-ALL</p><p style="clear: left;">"towards the house"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>It is also used with numerals and the question word <i>qassit</i> to express the time of the clock and in the meaning "amount per unit":
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">qassi-nut?</p><p style="margin: 0px;">when-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="allative case (&#39;to&#39;)" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ALL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">–</p><p style="margin: 0px;">&#160;</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">pingasu-nut.</p><p style="margin: 0px;">three-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="allative case (&#39;to&#39;)" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ALL</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">qassi-nut? – pingasu-nut.</p><p style="display: none;">when-ALL {} three-ALL</p><p style="clear: left;">"When?" – "At three o'clock"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">kiilu-mut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">kilo-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="allative case (&#39;to&#39;)" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ALL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">tiiva</p><p style="margin: 0px;">twenty</p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">krone-qar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">crown-have-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">kiilu-mut tiiva krone-qar-poq</p><p style="display: none;">kilo-ALL twenty crown-have-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"It costs 20 crowns per kilo"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Locative_case" title="Locative case">locative case</a> describes spatial location:<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase-104">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">illu-mi</p><p style="margin: 0px;">house-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="locative case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">LOC</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">illu-mi</p><p style="display: none;">house-LOC</p><p style="clear: left;">"in the house"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Ablative_case" title="Ablative case">ablative case</a> describes movement away from something or the source of something:<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase_104-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase-104">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Rasmussi-mit</p><p style="margin: 0px;">Rasmus-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="ablative case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">ABL</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">allagarsi-voq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">receive.letter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Rasmussi-mit allagarsi-voq</p><p style="display: none;">Rasmus-ABL receive.letter-3sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"He got a letter from Rasmus"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prosecutive_case" class="mw-redirect" title="Prosecutive case">prosecutive case</a> describes movement through something and the medium of writing or a location on the body.<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase2_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase2-105">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">matu-kkut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">door-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="prosecutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PROS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">iser-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">enter-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">matu-kkut iser-poq</p><p style="display: none;">door-PROS enter-3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"He entered through the door"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">su-kkut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">where-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="prosecutive case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">PROS</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">tillup-paatit?</p><p style="margin: 0px;">hit-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular">3sg</abbr>/<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="second person, singular">2sg</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">su-kkut tillup-paatit?</p><p style="display: none;">where-PROS hit-3sg/2sg</p><p style="clear: left;">"Where (on the body) did he hit you?"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The prosecutive case ending "-kkut" is distinct from the affix "-kkut" which denotes a noun and its companions, e.g. a person and friends or family(<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase3_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase3-106">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>):
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">palasi-kkut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">priest-and-companions-of</p></div><p style="display: none;">palasi-kkut</p><p style="display: none;">priest-and-companions-of</p><p style="clear: left;">"the priest and his family"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Equative_case" title="Equative case">equative case</a> describes similarity of manner or quality. It is also used to derive language names from nouns denoting nationalities: "like a person of x nationality [speaks]".<sup id="cite_ref-BjornumCase2_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BjornumCase2-105">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">nakorsatut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">doctor-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="equative case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">EQU</abbr></p></div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">suli-sar-poq</p><p style="margin: 0px;">work-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="habitual aspect" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">HAB</abbr>-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="third person, singular" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">3SG</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">nakorsatut suli-sar-poq</p><p style="display: none;">doctor-EQU work-HAB-3SG</p><p style="clear: left;">"he works as a doctor"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<div class="interlinear" style="margin-left:4em"><div style="position:absolute;left:1em">ex:</div><div style="float: left; margin-bottom: 0.3em;margin-right: 1em;"><p lang="kl" style="margin: 0px;font-style: italic;">Qallunaa-tut</p><p style="margin: 0px;">dane-<abbr class="gloss-abbr" title="equative case" style="font-variant: small-caps; font-variant-numeric: oldstyle-nums; text-transform: lowercase;">EQU</abbr></p></div><p style="display: none;">Qallunaa-tut</p><p style="display: none;">dane-EQU</p><p style="clear: left;">"Danish language (like a Dane)"</p><div style="clear: left; display: block;"></div>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Possession">Possession</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenlandic_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Possession"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="wikitable" style="margin: 0 0 0 1em; float: right;">
<caption>4. Absolutive possessive inflection for weak nouns
</caption>
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2">Possessor
